5/11/22, 13:09 - Sharmi: Dear All

Greetings from Indian Institute of Information Technology, Nagpur. We are delighted to inform you that IIC is organizing an online expert talk on â€œAdvancement in Defence Technologiesâ€ on the occasion of National Technology Day for Students and Faculties.
The details of the activity are as follows:
Speaker: Dr. Ravindra Singh, Director, Directorate of Parliamentary Affairs (DPA), DRDO.
Session on: Advancement in Defence Technology
Wednesday, May 11th, 2022, 1.00 to 2.00 PM (online mode).
Registration Link:  https://tinyurl.com/d85twrvy
Meeting Details:  https://iiitn.webex.com/iiitn/onstage/g.php?MTID=e5bc04e3c2b4c921fe5669ab673d6559c
Event number: 2512 299 9235
Event password: KVh3pkKZU69
The details of the speaker

Dr. Ravindra singh, Scientist 'G' and Director took over the office of Parliamentary Affairs, Official Language and Organization Method on 01 November 2019. He obtained his Master's degree in Electrical Engineering from IIT Roorkee in 1991 and soon after was appointed to Tata Consulting Engineers. After a brief stint there, joined DRDO in April 1992. His first appointment in DRDO was as Scientist 'B' at NSTL Visakhapatnam. There he played an important role in giving new direction to state-of-art Electrical Propulsion for Under-Water-Weapon-System Development. He Joined IRDE Dehradun in June 1996 after transfer from Visakhapatnam. Here, he made incomparable contribution in developing the indigenous Integrated Fire-Control-System consisting of Gunner's Main sighting system & Commanders panoramic sight for MBT Arjun and Electro-optical sighting equipment for Cheetah -Nag system.


He Worked at various levels in the LASTEC (Laser Science & Technology Centre) Delhi from 2001 to 2018. He made excellent contributions as Team Leader, Project Leader and Project Director in the design and development of High-Power Laser Weapon Systems and Laser Based Equipments. He developed various state-of-the-art technologies like Precision Laser Beam Control, Laser Cross Section Measurement etc. He Played an unprecedented role in developing the Space Qualified Indigenous Laser-Transmitter for ISRO's Chandrayaan Mission.  He Served his distinguished services from February 2018 to October 30, 2019 as the Head of Budget and Audit division of DFMM Directorate of DRDO Headquarters.


He received DRDO's Agni Award as a team member in 1998 and 2013. He also Received Technology Group Award in 2003, 2010, 2013 and 2018. He was awarded the Scientist of the Year Award twice at the laboratory level in 2007 and 2015. His technical research papers have been published in 10 International Journals. In addition, more than 25 research papers have been published in various national and international conferences. At present there are 4 patents in his credit, out of which 01 has been approved and other 03 are under process.



Thanks and Regards

Dr. Rashmi A. Pandhare
